```javascript
class AuthService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = '/api/auth';
        this.token = localStorage.getItem('token');
    }

    async login(credentials) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/login`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify(credentials)
            });

            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Falha na autenticação');

            const data = await response.json();
            this.setToken(data.token);
            return data;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    setToken(token) {
        this.token = token;
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
    }

    getToken() {
        return this.token;
    }

    isAuthenticated() {
        return !!this.token;
    }

    logout() {
        this.token = null;
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
    }
}

export default new AuthService();
```

```javascript
class UserManager {
    constructor() {
        this.users = new Map();
    }

    async createUser(userData) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/users', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${AuthService.getToken()}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(userData)
            });

            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Erro ao criar usuário');
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async getUser(id) {
        if (this.users.has(id)) {
            return this.users.get(id);
        }

        const response = await fetch(`/api/users/${id}`);
        const user = await response.json();
        this.users.set(id, user);
        return user;
    }
}

export default new UserManager();
```

```javascript
class ApiClient {
    constructor(baseURL) {
        this.baseURL = baseURL;
        this.headers = new Headers({
            'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    setAuthToken(token) {
        if (token) {
            this.headers.set('Authorization', `Bearer ${token}`);
        } else {
            this.headers.delete('Authorization');
        }
    }

    async request(endpoint, options = {}) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseURL}${endpoint}`, {
                ...options,
                headers: this.headers
            });

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
            }

            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('API request failed:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    get(endpoint) {
        return this.request(endpoint);
    }

    post(endpoint, data) {
        return this.request(endpoint, {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
    }

    put(endpoint, data) {
        return this.request(endpoint, {
            method: 'PUT',
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
    }

    delete(endpoint) {
        return this.request(endpoint, {
            method: 'DELETE'
        });
    }
}

export default new ApiClient('http://localhost:3000/api');
```

```javascript
class TestRunner {
    constructor() {
        this.tests = new Map();
        this.results = [];
    }

    addTest(name, testFn) {
        this.tests.set(name, testFn);
    }

    async runTests() {
        for (const [name, test] of this.tests) {
            try {
                await test();
                this.results.push({
                    name,
                    status: 'passed'
                });
            } catch (error) {
                this.results.push({
                    name,
                    status: 'failed',
                    error: error.message
                });
            }
        }
        return this.results;
    }

    generateReport() {
        const total = this.results.length;
        const passed = this.results.filter(r => r.status === 'passed').length;
        
        return {
            total,
            passed,
            failed: total - passed,
            details: this.results
        };
    }
}
```

```javascript
class FileManager {
    constructor() {
        this.supportedTypes = ['pdf', 'doc', 'docx', 'jpg', 'png'];
    }

    async saveFile(file, path) {
        try {
            const extension = file.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            if (!this.supportedTypes.includes(extension)) {
                throw new Error('Tipo de arquivo não suportado');
            }

            const response = await fetch('/api/files/upload', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: this.createFormData(file, path)
            });

            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Erro ao salvar arquivo');
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no gerenciamento de arquivo:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    createFormData(file, path) {
        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('file', file);
        formData.append('path', path);
        return formData;
    }

    async getFile(fileId) {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/files/${fileId}`);
        if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Arquivo não encontrado');
        return await response.blob();
    }
}

export default new FileManager();
```

```javascript
class PrintService {
    constructor() {
        this.printerOptions = {
            format: 'A4',
            orientation: 'portrait',
            margin: {
                top: '20mm',
                bottom: '20mm',
                left: '20mm',
                right: '20mm'
            }
        };
    }

    async printDocument(content, options = {}) {
        const mergedOptions = { ...this.printerOptions, ...options };
        
        try {
            const printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
            printWindow.document.write(`
                <!DOCTYPE html>
                <html>
                <head>
                    <title>Impressão</title>
                    <style>
                        @page {
                            size: ${mergedOptions.format} ${mergedOptions.orientation};
                            margin: ${mergedOptions.margin.top} ${mergedOptions.margin.right} 
                                    ${mergedOptions.margin.bottom} ${mergedOptions.margin.left};
                        }
                        body {
                            font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
                            line-height: 1.6;
                        }
                    </style>
                </head>
                <body>
                    ${content}
                </body>
                </html>
            `);
            
            printWindow.document.close();
            printWindow.focus();
            printWindow.print();
            printWindow.close();
            
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro na impressão:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async previewDocument(content, options = {}) {
        // Preview implementation
    }

    async getPrinterList() {
        // Get available printers
    }
}

export default new PrintService();
```

```javascript
class ReportManager {
    constructor() {
        this.templates = new Map();
        this.exportService = new ExportService();
        this.emailService = new EmailService();
    }

    registerTemplate(name, template) {
        this.templates.set(name, template);
    }

    async generateReport(templateName, data) {
        const template = this.templates.get(templateName);
        if (!template) {
            throw new Error(`Template ${templateName} não encontrado`);
        }

        const report = await template(data);
        return {
            content: report,
            export: async (format) => this.exportService.export(report, format),
            send: async (email) => this.emailService.sendReport(report, email)
        };
    }
}
```

```javascript
class NotificationService {
    constructor() {
        this.channels = new Map();
        this.subscribers = new Set();
        this.templates = {
            appointment: {
                title: "Novo Agendamento",
                body: (data) => `Olá ${data.patientName}, 
                    sua consulta foi agendada para ${data.date} às ${data.time}`
            }
        };
    }

    subscribe(channel, callback) {
        if (!this.channels.has(channel)) {
            this.channels.set(channel, new Set());
        }
        this.channels.get(channel).add(callback);
    }

    async notify(channel, data) {
        if (!this.channels.has(channel)) return;
        
        const callbacks = this.channels.get(channel);
        const template = this.templates[channel];
        
        if (template) {
            const message = {
                title: template.title,
                body: template.body(data),
                timestamp: new Date()
            };

            callbacks.forEach(callback => callback(message));
        }
    }
}
```

```javascript

            await this.notificationService.notify('appointment', {

                time: appointment.time

            return appointment;

            console.error('Erro ao criar agendamento:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

}
```

```javascript
class DocumentManager {
    constructor() {
        this.documents = new Map();
        this.templates = {
            patientRecord: (data) => this.createPatientRecord(data),
            prescription: (data) => this.createPrescription(data)
        };
    }

    async createPatientRecord(data) {
        return {
            type: 'patient-record',
            content: `
                <div class="patient-record">
                    <h1>Prontuário do Paciente</h1>
                    <div class="patient-info">
                        <p>Nome: ${data.name}</p>
                        <p>CPF: ${data.cpf}</p>
                        <p>Data Nascimento: ${data.birthDate}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="medical-history">
                        ${this.formatMedicalHistory(data.history)}
                    </div>
                </div>
            `
        };
    }

    formatMedicalHistory(history) {
        return history.map(item => `
            <div class="history-item">
                <p>Data: ${item.date}</p>
                <p>Descrição: ${item.description}</p>
                <p>Profissional: ${item.professional}</p>
            </div>
        `).join('');
    }
}
```

```javascript
class PatientManager {

        this.patients = new Map();
        this.documentManager = new DocumentManager();
    }

    async createPatient(patientData) {
        try {
            const patient = await this.savePatient(patientData);
            await this.documentManager.createPatientRecord(patient);
            return patient;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao criar paciente:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async getPatientHistory(patientId) {
        try {
            const patient = await this.getPatient(patientId);
            return patient.history || [];
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao buscar histórico:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }
}
```

```javascript
class BaseService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = process.env.API_URL || 'http://localhost:3000/api';
        this.headers = new Headers({
            'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    async request(endpoint, options = {}) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}${endpoint}`, {
                ...options,
                headers: this.headers
            });

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error(`Erro HTTP: ${response.status}`);
            }

            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro na requisição:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    setAuthToken(token) {
        if (token) {
            this.headers.set('Authorization', `Bearer ${token}`);
        } else {
            this.headers.delete('Authorization');
        }
    }
}
```

```javascript
class ClientService extends BaseService {
    constructor() {
        super();
        this.endpoint = '/clients';
    }

    async getAll() {
        return this.request(this.endpoint);
    }

    async getById(id) {
        return this.request(`${this.endpoint}/${id}`);
    }

    async create(data) {
        return this.request(this.endpoint, {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
    }

    async update(id, data) {
        return this.request(`${this.endpoint}/${id}`, {
            method: 'PUT',
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
    }

    async delete(id) {
        return this.request(`${this.endpoint}/${id}`, {
            method: 'DELETE'
        });
    }
}

export default new ClientService();
```

```batch
mkdir clinica-sistema
cd clinica-sistema
mkdir src\services src\components src\utils src\assets
code .
```

```javascript
class BaseService {
    constructor() {
        this.config = {
            apiUrl: process.env.API_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
            timeout: 5000
        };
        this.initialize();
    }

    initialize() {
        this.headers = new Headers({
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            'Accept': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    async request(endpoint, options = {}) {
        const controller = new AbortController();
        const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), this.config.timeout);

        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.config.apiUrl}${endpoint}`, {
                ...options,
                headers: this.headers,
                signal: controller.signal
            });

            clearTimeout(timeoutId);

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error(`HTTP Error: ${response.status}`);
            }

            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            if (error.name === 'AbortError') {
                throw new Error('Requisição excedeu o tempo limite');
            }
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

export default BaseService;
```

```javascript
import BaseService from './BaseService';

class AuthService extends BaseService {
    constructor() {
        super();
        this.endpoint = '/auth';
    }

    async login(credentials) {
        return this.request(`${this.endpoint}/login`, {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify(credentials)
        });
    }

    async logout() {
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
        this.headers.delete('Authorization');
    }

    setToken(token) {
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
        this.headers.set('Authorization', `Bearer ${token}`);
    }
}

export default new AuthService();
```

```javascript
class ApiService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseURL = process.env.API_URL || 'http://localhost:3000';
        this.timeout = 5000;
        this.initialize();
    }

    initialize() {
        this.headers = new Headers({
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            'Accept': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    async request(endpoint, options = {}) {
        const controller = new AbortController();
        const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), this.timeout);

        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseURL}${endpoint}`, {
                ...options,
                headers: this.headers,
                signal: controller.signal
            });

            clearTimeout(timeoutId);

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error(`Erro HTTP: ${response.status}`);
            }

            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            if (error.name === 'AbortError') {
                throw new Error('Timeout da requisição');
            }
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

export default new ApiService();
```

```javascript
import ApiService from '../services/ApiService';

describe('ApiService', () => {
    test('deve fazer requisição com sucesso', async () => {
        const response = await ApiService.request('/test');
        expect(response).toBeDefined();
    });

    test('deve lançar erro em timeout', async () => {
        await expect(ApiService.request('/timeout')).rejects.toThrow('Timeout');
    });
```

```javascript
class UserService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = '/api/users';
        this.headers = new Headers({
            'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    async getUser(id) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/${id}`, {
                headers: this.headers
            });
            
            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error('Usuário não encontrado');
            }

            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao buscar usuário:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async updateUser(id, data) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/${id}`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: this.headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(data)
            });

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error('Erro ao atualizar usuário');
            }

            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro na atualização:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

export default new UserService();
```

```javascript
class AuthService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = '/api/auth';
        this.token = localStorage.getItem('token');
        this.user = null;
    }

    async login(credentials) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/login`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(credentials)
            });

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error('Credenciais inválidas');
            }

            const data = await response.json();
            this.setToken(data.token);
            this.user = data.user;
            return data;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    setToken(token) {
        this.token = token;
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
    }

    getUser() {
        return this.user;
    }

    isAuthenticated() {
        return !!this.token;
    }

    logout() {
        this.token = null;
        this.user = null;
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
    }
}

export default new AuthService();
```

Aguarde para continuar com a próxima implementação.

```javascript
            'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    async getPatients() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(this.baseUrl, {
                headers: this.headers
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao buscar pacientes:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async createPatient(data) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(this.baseUrl, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: this.headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(data)
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao criar paciente:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async updatePatient(id, data) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/${id}`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: this.headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(data)
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao atualizar paciente:', error);
```

```javascript
class Database {
    constructor() {
        this.config = {
            host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
            user: process.env.DB_USER || 'root',
            password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
            database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'clinica'
        };
    }

    async connect() {
        try {
            const mysql = require('mysql2/promise');
            this.connection = await mysql.createConnection(this.config);
            console.log('Database connected');
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Database connection error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async query(sql, params = []) {
        try {
            const [results] = await this.connection.execute(sql, params);
            return results;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Query error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

export default new Database();
```

```javascript
class AppointmentService {
    constructor() {
        this.db = require('../database/Database');
    }

    async createAppointment(data) {
        const sql = `
            INSERT INTO appointments 
            (patient_id, date, time, type, status) 
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
        `;
        
        const params = [
            data.patientId,
            data.date,
            data.time,
            data.type,
            'scheduled'
        ];

        return await this.db.query(sql, params);
    }

    async getAppointments(filters = {}) {
        const sql = `
            SELECT a.*, p.name as patient_name 
            FROM appointments a
            JOIN patients p ON a.patient_id = p.id
            WHERE a.date >= ?
        `;

        return await this.db.query(sql, [new Date()]);
    }
}

export default new AppointmentService();
```

```javascript
import mysql from 'mysql2/promise';
import config from '../database/config';

class DatabaseService {
    constructor() {
        this.config = config;
        this.connection = null;
    }

    async connect() {
        try {
            this.connection = await mysql.createConnection(this.config);
            console.log('Database connected successfully');
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Database connection error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async query(sql, params = []) {
        if (!this.connection) {
            await this.connect();
        }

        try {
            const [results] = await this.connection.execute(sql, params);
            return results;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Query error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

export default new DatabaseService();
```

```javascript
class BaseService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = process.env.API_URL || 'http://localhost:3000';
        this.headers = new Headers({
            'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    async request(endpoint, options = {}) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}${endpoint}`, {
                ...options,
                headers: this.headers
            });

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error(`HTTP Error: ${response.status}`);
            }

            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Request error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    setAuthToken(token) {
        if (token) {
            this.headers.set('Authorization', `Bearer ${token}`);
        } else {
            this.headers.delete('Authorization');
        }
    }
}

export default BaseService;
```

```javascript
import BaseService from './BaseService';

class AppointmentService extends BaseService {
    constructor() {
        super();
        this.endpoint = '/appointments';
    }

    async getAppointments(filters = {}) {
        const queryString = new URLSearchParams(filters).toString();
        return this.request(`${this.endpoint}?${queryString}`);
    }

    async createAppointment(data) {
        return this.request(this.endpoint, {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
    }

    async updateAppointment(id, data) {
        return this.request(`${this.endpoint}/${id}`, {
            method: 'PUT',
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
    }

    async deleteAppointment(id) {
        return this.request(`${this.endpoint}/${id}`, {
            method: 'DELETE'
        });
    }
}

export default new AppointmentService();
```

```javascript
class DatabaseService {
    constructor() {
        this.config = {
            host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
            user: process.env.DB_USER || 'root',
            password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
            database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'clinica'
        };
        this.pool = null;
    }

    async connect() {
        if (!this.pool) {
            const mysql = require('mysql2/promise');
            this.pool = mysql.createPool(this.config);
        }
        return this.pool;
    }

    async query(sql, params = []) {
        const connection = await this.connect();
        try {
            const [results] = await connection.execute(sql, params);
            return results;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro na consulta:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async transaction(callback) {
        const connection = await this.connect();
        try {
            await connection.beginTransaction();
            const result = await callback(connection);
            await connection.commit();
            return result;
        } catch (error) {
            await connection.rollback();
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

export default new DatabaseService();
```

```javascript
class AuthService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = '/api/auth';
        this.token = localStorage.getItem('token');
    }

    async login(credentials) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/login`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify(credentials)
            });

            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Credenciais inválidas');

            const data = await response.json();
            this.setToken(data.token);
            return data;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    setToken(token) {
        this.token = token;
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
    }

    isAuthenticated() {
        return !!this.token;
    }

    logout() {
        this.token = null;
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
    }
}

export default new AuthService();
```

```javascript
const mysql = require('mysql2/promise');

class Database {
    constructor() {
        this.config = {
            host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
            user: process.env.DB_USER || 'root',
            password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
            database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'clinica',
            waitForConnections: true,
            connectionLimit: 10,
            queueLimit: 0
        };
        this.pool = null;
    }

    async getConnection() {
        if (!this.pool) {
            this.pool = mysql.createPool(this.config);
        }
        return this.pool;
    }

    async query(sql, params = []) {
        const connection = await this.getConnection();
        try {
            const [results] = await connection.execute(sql, params);
            return results;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Database error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new Database();
```

```javascript
class ApiService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = process.env.API_URL || 'http://localhost:3000/api';
        this.headers = new Headers({
            'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    async request(endpoint, options = {}) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}${endpoint}`, {
                ...options,
                headers: this.headers
            });

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error(`HTTP Error: ${response.status}`);
            }

            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('API Error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    setAuthToken(token) {
        if (token) {
            this.headers.set('Authorization', `Bearer ${token}`);
        } else {
            this.headers.delete('Authorization');
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new ApiService();
```

```javascript
class Dashboard {
    constructor() {
        this.state = {
            agendamentosHoje: [],
            pacientesAtivos: 0,
            proximasConsultas: []
        };
        this.init();
    }

    async init() {
        await this.carregarDados();
        this.render();
        this.bindEvents();
    }

    async carregarDados() {
        try {
            const [agendamentos, pacientes, consultas] = await Promise.all([
                fetch('/api/agendamentos/hoje'),
                fetch('/api/pacientes/ativos'),
                fetch('/api/consultas/proximas')
            ]);

            this.setState({
                agendamentosHoje: await agendamentos.json(),
                pacientesAtivos: await pacientes.json(),
                proximasConsultas: await consultas.json()
            });
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao carregar dashboard:', error);
        }
    }

    setState(newState) {
        this.state = { ...this.state, ...newState };
        this.render();
    }

    render() {
        const template = `
            <div class="dashboard">
                <div class="dashboard-header">
                    <h1>Painel de Controle</h1>
                </div>
                <div class="dashboard-grid">
                    ${this.renderAgendamentosHoje()}
                    ${this.renderPacientesAtivos()}
                    ${this.renderProximasConsultas()}
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        document.getElementById('app').innerHTML = template;
    }

    bindEvents() {
        // Implementar eventos do dashboard
    }
}

export default Dashboard;
```

#### Implementação da Agenda:

```javascript
class Agenda {
    constructor() {
        this.state = {
            eventos: [],
            dataAtual: new Date(),
            visualizacao: 'semana'
        };
        this.init();
    }

    async init() {
        await this.carregarEventos();
        this.render();
        this.bindEvents();
    }

    async carregarEventos() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/eventos');
            this.setState({ eventos: await response.json() });
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao carregar eventos:', error);
        }
    }

    setState(newState) {
        this.state = { ...this.state, ...newState };
        this.render();
    }

    render() {
        const template = `
            <div class="agenda">
                <div class="agenda-header">
                    <button class="btn-anterior">&lt;</button>
                    <h2>${this.formatarData(this.state.dataAtual)}</h2>
                    <button class="btn-proximo">&gt;</button>
                </div>
                <div class="agenda-grid">
                    ${this.renderEventos()}
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        document.getElementById('app').innerHTML = template;
    }

    renderEventos() {
        return this.state.eventos
            .map(evento => `
                <div class="evento" data-id="${evento.id}">
                    <span class="hora">${evento.hora}</span>
                    <span class="titulo">${evento.titulo}</span>
                </div>
            `)
            .join('');
    }

    bindEvents() {
        document.querySelector('.btn-anterior').addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.navegarData(-1);
        });

        document.querySelector('.btn-proximo').addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.navegarData(1);
        });
    }

    navegarData(direcao) {
        const novaData = new Date(this.state.dataAtual);
        novaData.setDate(novaData.getDate() + direcao);
        this.setState({ dataAtual: novaData });
        this.carregarEventos();
    }

    formatarData(data) {
        return data.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
    }
}

export default Agenda;
```

```javascript
class ProntuarioService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = '/api/prontuarios';
        this.headers = new Headers({
            'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        });
    }

    async getProntuario(pacienteId) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/${pacienteId}`, {
                headers: this.headers
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao buscar prontuário:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async salvarProntuario(prontuario) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(this.baseUrl, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: this.headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(prontuario)
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao salvar prontuário:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async atualizarProntuario(id, dados) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/${id}`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: this.headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(dados)
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao atualizar prontuário:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

export default new ProntuarioService();
```

Aguarde para continuar com os próximos componentes do sistema.

```javascript
class NotificationService {
    constructor() {
        this.providers = {
            whatsapp: new WhatsAppProvider(),
            email: new EmailProvider()
        };
    }

    async sendNotification(type, data) {
        try {
            switch(type) {
                case 'appointment':
                    await this.sendAppointmentNotification(data);
                    break;
                case 'reminder':
                    await this.sendReminderNotification(data);
                    break;
                default:
                    throw new Error('Tipo de notificação inválido');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao enviar notificação:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async sendAppointmentNotification(data) {
        const message = `
            Olá ${data.patientName},
            Seu agendamento foi confirmado para:
            Data: ${data.date}
            Hora: ${data.time}
        `;

        await this.providers.whatsapp.send(data.phone, message);
        await this.providers.email.send(data.email, 'Confirmação de Agendamento', message);
    }
}
```

```javascript
class ReportGenerator {
    constructor() {
        this.templates = new Map();
        this.initializeTemplates();
    }

    initializeTemplates() {
        this.templates.set('clinical', this.clinicalTemplate);
        this.templates.set('financial', this.financialTemplate);
    }

    async generateReport(type, data) {
        const template = this.templates.get(type);
        if (!template) throw new Error('Template não encontrado');
        
        const report = template(data);
        return {
            content: report,
            timestamp: new Date(),
            type
        };
    }

    async exportPDF(report) {
        // Implementação da exportação PDF
    }
}
```

```javascript
class FileSystemService {
    constructor() {
        this.fs = require('fs/promises');
        this.path = require('path');
        this.baseDir = process.env.FILES_DIR || './files';
    }

    async createDirectory(dirPath) {
        const fullPath = this.path.join(this.baseDir, dirPath);
        await this.fs.mkdir(fullPath, { recursive: true });
        return fullPath;
    }

    async saveFile(filePath, content) {
        const fullPath = this.path.join(this.baseDir, filePath);
        await this.fs.writeFile(fullPath, content);
        return fullPath;
    }

    async getFile(filePath) {
        const fullPath = this.path.join(this.baseDir, filePath);
        return await this.fs.readFile(fullPath);
    }
}

export default new FileSystemService();
```

```javascript
class LoggerService {
    constructor() {
        this.logs = [];
        this.maxLogs = 1000;
    }

    log(level, message, metadata = {}) {
        const logEntry = {
            timestamp: new Date(),
            level,
            message,
            metadata
        };

        this.logs.push(logEntry);
        if (this.logs.length > this.maxLogs) {
            this.archive();
        }

        console.log(`[${level}] ${message}`);
    }

    async archive() {
        // Implementar arquivamento de logs
    }
}

export default new LoggerService();
```

```javascript
class TestRunner {
    constructor() {
        this.tests = new Map();
        this.results = [];
    }

    addTest(name, testFn) {
        this.tests.set(name, testFn);
    }

    async runTests() {
        for (const [name, test] of this.tests) {
            try {
                await test();
                this.results.push({
                    name,
                    status: 'passed'
                });
            } catch (error) {
                this.results.push({
                    name,
                    status: 'failed',
                    error: error.message
                });
            }
        }
        return this.generateReport();
    }

    generateReport() {
        const total = this.results.length;
        const passed = this.results.filter(r => r.status === 'passed').length;
        const failed = total - passed;

        return {
            total,
            passed,
            failed,
            details: this.results
        };
    }
}
```

```javascript
class DocsGenerator {
    constructor() {
        this.docs = new Map();
    }

    addDoc(path, content) {
        this.docs.set(path, content);
    }

    async generateDocs() {
        const markdown = [];
        for (const [path, content] of this.docs) {
            markdown.push(`## ${path}\n\n${content}\n`);
        }
        return markdown.join('\n');
    }

    async exportDocs(format = 'md') {
        const content = await this.generateDocs();
        // Implementar exportação
        return content;
    }
}
```

```javascript
class ConfigService {
    constructor() {
        this.config = {
            development: {
                database: {
                    host: 'localhost',
                    port: 3306,
                    user: 'root',
                    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
                    database: 'clinica_dev'
                },
                api: {
                    port: 3000,
                    cors: true
                }
            },
            production: {
                database: {
                    host: process.env.DB_HOST,
                    port: process.env.DB_PORT,
                    user: process.env.DB_USER,
                    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
                    database: process.env.DB_NAME
                },
                api: {
                    port: process.env.API_PORT,
                    cors: false
                }
            }
        };
    }

    getConfig(env = process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development') {
        return this.config[env];
    }
}

export default new ConfigService();
```

```javascript
class DeployService {
    constructor() {
        this.steps = [
            this.backupDatabase,
            this.updateCode,
            this.migrateDatabase,
            this.restartServices
        ];
    }

    async deploy() {
        try {
            for (const step of this.steps) {
                await step();
            }
            console.log('Deploy concluído com sucesso');
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no deploy:', error);
            await this.rollback();
        }
    }

    async updateCode() {
        // Implementação da atualização do código

    async migrateDatabase() {
        // Implementação da migração do banco
    }

    async restartServices() {
        // Implementação do restart dos serviços
    }

}
```

```javascript
class MetricsCollector {
    constructor() {
        this.metrics = {
            systemStats: [],
            applicationStats: [],
            databaseStats: []
        };
        this.intervalId = null;
    }

    startCollection() {
        this.intervalId = setInterval(() => {
            this.collect();
        }, 5000);
    }

    async collect() {
        try {
            const stats = {
                timestamp: new Date(),
                system: await this.getSystemStats(),
                application: await this.getApplicationStats(),
                database: await this.getDatabaseStats()
            };

            await this.saveMetrics(stats);
            await this.checkThresholds(stats);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro na coleta de métricas:', error);
        }
    }

    async getSystemStats() {
        return {
            cpu: process.cpuUsage(),
            memory: process.memoryUsage(),
            uptime: process.uptime()
        };
    }

    async saveMetrics(stats) {
        // Implementar salvamento no banco
    }
}

export default new MetricsCollector();
```

```javascript
class SystemMonitor {
    constructor() {
        this.metrics = new MetricsCollector();
        this.alerts = new AlertSystem();
        this.dashboard = new DashboardUpdater();
    }

    async initialize() {
        await this.metrics.start();
        await this.alerts.initialize();
        await this.dashboard.start();
        
        this.startMonitoring();
    }

    startMonitoring() {
        setInterval(async () => {
            const systemMetrics = await this.metrics.collect();
            await this.alerts.check(systemMetrics);
            await this.dashboard.update(systemMetrics);
        }, 30000);
    }
}

export default new SystemMonitor();
```

```javascript
class MetricsCollector {
    constructor() {
        this.data = [];
        this.maxDataPoints = 1000;
    }

    async collect() {
        const metrics = {
            timestamp: new Date(),
            memory: process.memoryUsage(),
            cpu: await this.getCPUUsage(),
            disk: await this.getDiskUsage(),
            network: await this.getNetworkStats()
        };

        this.data.push(metrics);
        if (this.data.length > this.maxDataPoints) {
            this.data.shift();
        }

        return metrics;
    }
}

export default MetricsCollector;
```

```javascript
class MonitoringService {

        this.metrics = {
            performance: [],
            resources: [],
            errors: []
        };
        this.config = {
            interval: 30000,
            maxDataPoints: 1000
        };
    }

    async start() {
        setInterval(async () => {
            await this.collectMetrics();
            await this.analyzeMetrics();
            await this.updateDashboard();
        }, this.config.interval);
    }

    async collectMetrics() {
        const metrics = {
            timestamp: new Date(),
            performance: await this.getPerformanceMetrics(),
            resources: await this.getResourceMetrics(),
            errors: await this.getErrorLogs()
        };

        this.storeMetrics(metrics);
    }

    async getPerformanceMetrics() {
        return {
            cpu: process.cpuUsage(),
            memory: process.memoryUsage(),
            requests: await this.getRequestStats()
        };
    }
```

```sql
CREATE TABLE patients (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE appointments (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    patient_id INT,
    date_time DATETIME,
    status VARCHAR(20),
    FOREIGN KEY (patient_id) REFERENCES patients(id)
);
```

```javascript
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
import Dashboard from './Dashboard';
import Appointments from './Appointments';
import Patients from './Patients';

function App() {
    const [isAuthenticated, setIsAuthenticated] = useState(false);

    useEffect(() => {
        checkAuth();
    }, []);

    const checkAuth = async () => {
        const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
        if (token) {
            setIsAuthenticated(true);
        }
    };

    return (
        <BrowserRouter>
            <Routes>
                <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
                <Route path="/appointments" element={<Appointments />} />
                <Route path="/patients" element={<Patients />} />
            </Routes>
        </BrowserRouter>
    );
}

export default App;
```

```javascript
.js
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const mysql = require('mysql2/promise');

const app = express();
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());

const db = mysql.createPool({
    host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
    user: process.env.DB_USER || 'root',
    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
    database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'clinica'
});

app.listen(3000, () => {
    console.log('Servidor rodando na porta 3000');
});
```

```javascript
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Card, Grid, Typography } from '@material-ui/core';
import { useApi } from '../hooks/useApi';

const Dashboard = () => {
    const [stats, setStats] = useState({
        totalPatients: 0,
        todayAppointments: 0,
        pendingPayments: 0
    });
    const api = useApi();

    useEffect(() => {
        loadDashboardData();
    }, []);

    const loadDashboardData = async () => {
        try {
            const response = await api.get('/dashboard/stats');
            setStats(response.data);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao carregar dashboard:', error);
        }
    };

    return (
        <Grid container spacing={3}>
            <Grid item xs={12} md={4}>
                <Card>
                    <Typography variant="h6">Total de Pacientes</Typography>
                    <Typography variant="h4">{stats.totalPatients}</Typography>
                </Card>
            </Grid>
            {/* Outros cards do dashboard */}
        </Grid>
    );
};

export default Dashboard;
```

```javascript
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { DataGrid } from '@material-ui/data-grid';
import { api } from '../services/api';

const AppointmentsGrid = () => {
    const [appointments, setAppointments] = useState([]);
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

    const columns = [
        { field: 'id', headerName: 'ID', width: 90 },
        { field: 'patientName', headerName: 'Paciente', width: 200 },
        { field: 'date', headerName: 'Data', width: 130 },
        { field: 'time', headerName: 'Horário', width: 130 },
        { field: 'status', headerName: 'Status', width: 130 }
    ];

    useEffect(() => {
        loadAppointments();
    }, []);

    const loadAppointments = async () => {
        setLoading(true);
        try {
            const response = await api.get('/appointments');
            setAppointments(response.data);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao carregar agendamentos:', error);
        } finally {
            setLoading(false);
        }
    };

    return (
        <div style={{ height: 400, width: '100%' }}>
            <DataGrid
                rows={appointments}
                columns={columns}
                pageSize={10}
                loading={loading}
                autoHeight
            />
        </div>
    );
};

export default AppointmentsGrid;
```

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const db = require('../database');

router.get('/', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const appointments = await db.query(`
            SELECT 
                a.id,
                p.name as patientName,
                a.date,
                a.time,
                a.status
            FROM appointments a
            JOIN patients p ON a.patient_id = p.id
            ORDER BY a.date DESC, a.time ASC
        `);
        res.json(appointments);
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
    }
});

module.exports = router;
```

```javascript
export interface Appointment {
    id: number;
    patientId: number;
    patientName: string;
    date: string;
    time: string;
    status: 'scheduled' | 'completed' | 'cancelled';
    createdAt: string;
    updatedAt: string;
}
```

#### Frontend - Autenticação:

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useState, useContext } from 'react';
import api from '../services/api';

export const AuthContext = createContext({});

export const AuthProvider = ({ children }) => {
    const [user, setUser] = useState(null);

    const login = async (credentials) => {
        try {
            const response = await api.post('/auth/login', credentials);
            setUser(response.data.user);
            localStorage.setItem('token', response.data.token);
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
            return false;
        }
    };

    const logout = () => {
        setUser(null);
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
    };

    return (
        <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, login, logout }}>
            {children}
        </AuthContext.Provider>
    );
};
```

#### Backend - Banco de Dados:

```sql
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS clinica;
USE clinica;

CREATE TABLE users (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    role ENUM('admin', 'doctor', 'staff') NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE patients (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    cpf VARCHAR(14) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    birth_date DATE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE appointments (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    patient_id INT,
    doctor_id INT,
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    time TIME NOT NULL,
    status ENUM('scheduled', 'completed', 'cancelled') DEFAULT 'scheduled',
    notes TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (patient_id) REFERENCES patients(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (doctor_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);
```

```sql
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS clinica;
USE clinica;

CREATE TABLE users (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    role ENUM('admin', 'doctor', 'staff') NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE patients (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    cpf VARCHAR(14) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    birth_date DATE,
    address TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE appointments (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    patient_id INT,
    doctor_id INT,
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    time TIME NOT NULL,
    status ENUM('scheduled', 'completed', 'cancelled') DEFAULT 'scheduled',
    notes TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (patient_id) REFERENCES patients(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (doctor_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);

CREATE TABLE medical_records (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    patient_id INT,
    doctor_id INT,
    appointment_id INT,
    description TEXT NOT NULL,
    prescription TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (patient_id) REFERENCES patients(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (doctor_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (appointment_id) REFERENCES appointments(id)
);
```

```javascript
class AuthService {
    constructor() {
        this.baseUrl = '/api/auth';
        this.token = localStorage.getItem('token');
    }

    async login(credentials) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/login`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify(credentials)
            });

            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Credenciais inválidas');

            const data = await response.json();
            this.setToken(data.token);
            return data;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    setToken(token) {
        this.token = token;
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
    }

    isAuthenticated() {
        return !!this.token;
    }

    logout() {
        this.token = null;
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
    }
}

export default new AuthService();
```

```sql
CREATE DATABASE clinica;
USE clinica;

CREATE TABLE usuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    senha VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    tipo ENUM('admin', 'medico', 'paciente') NOT NULL
);

    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    telefone VARCHAR(20),
    cpf VARCHAR(14) UNIQUE
);

CREATE TABLE agendamentos (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    data DATE,
    hora TIME,
    status ENUM('agendado', 'confirmado', 'cancelado'),
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id)
);
```

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // Sistema de autenticação
    const auth = {
        login: async (email, senha) => {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/login', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ email, senha })
                });
                return await response.json();
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Erro no login:', error);
            }
        }
    };

    // Sistema de agendamento
    const agendamento = {
        criar: async (data) => {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/agendamento', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify(data)
                });
                return await response.json();
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Erro no agendamento:', error);
            }
        }
    };
});
```

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const app = {
        init() {
            this.bindEvents();
        },

        bindEvents() {
            const menuLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.menu a');
            menuLinks.forEach(link => {
                link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const id = e.target.getAttribute('href').substring(1);
                    this.navegarPara(id);
                });
            });
        },

        navegarPara(id) {
            const secoes = document.querySelectorAll('section');
            secoes.forEach(secao => secao.classList.remove('secao-ativa'));
            document.getElementById(id).classList.add('secao-ativa');
        }
    };

    app.init();
});
```

```javascript
const auth = {
    async login(email, senha) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/login', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ email, senha })
            });
            
            if (response.ok) {
                const data = await response.json();
                localStorage.setItem('token', data.token);
                window.location.href = 'dashboard.html';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
        }
    }
};

document.getElementById('loginForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const email = document.getElementById('email').value;
    const senha = document.getElementById('senha').value;
    await auth.login(email, senha);
});
```

```javascript
const pacienteService = {
    async cadastrar(paciente) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/pacientes', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(paciente)
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao cadastrar paciente:', error);
        }
    },

    async listar() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/pacientes', {
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
                }
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao listar pacientes:', error);
        }
    }
};
```

```javascript
const agendamentoService = {
    async criar(agendamento) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/agendamentos', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(agendamento)
            });
            
            if (response.ok) {
                const data = await response.json();
                await this.enviarNotificacao(data);
                return data;
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no agendamento:', error);
        }
    },

    async enviarNotificacao(agendamento) {
        // Integração com WhatsApp/Email
        try {
            await fetch('/api/notificacoes', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    tipo: 'agendamento',
                    dados: agendamento
                })
            });
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao enviar notificação:', error);
        }
    }
};
```

```sql
-- Criar procedure para backup
DELIMITER //
CREATE PROCEDURE realizarBackup()
BEGIN
    SET @backup_path = 'C:/backups/';
    SET @backup_name = CONCAT('backup_', DATE_FORMAT(NOW(), '%Y%m%d_%H%i%s'), '.sql');
    SET @comando = CONCAT('mysqldump -u root -p clinica > ', @backup_path, @backup_name);
    
    -- Executar backup
    SET @resultado = sys_exec(@comando);
END //
DELIMITER ;

-- Agendar backup diário
CREATE EVENT backup_diario
    ON SCHEDULE EVERY 1 DAY
    DO CALL realizarBackup();
```

```javascript
const prontuarioService = {
    async criar(prontuario) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/prontuarios', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(prontuario)
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao criar prontuário:', error);
        }
    },

    async buscarPorPaciente(pacienteId) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`/api/prontuarios/${pacienteId}`, {
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
                }
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao buscar prontuário:', error);
        }
    }
};
```

GitHub Copilot: ### Plano de Implementação - Sistema Clínica

1. **Setup Inicial Windows**
```batch
REM filepath: /setup.bat
mkdir clinica
cd clinica
mkdir css js database pages
```

2. **Banco de Dados**
```sql
CREATE DATABASE clinica;
USE clinica;

CREATE TABLE usuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    senha VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    tipo ENUM('admin', 'medico', 'paciente') DEFAULT 'paciente'
);

CREATE TABLE pacientes (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    telefone VARCHAR(20),
    cpf VARCHAR(14) UNIQUE,
    data_nascimento DATE,
    endereco TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE agendamentos (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    medico_id INT,
    data DATE NOT NULL,
    hora TIME NOT NULL,
    status ENUM('pendente', 'confirmado', 'cancelado') DEFAULT 'pendente',
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (medico_id) REFERENCES usuarios(id)
);

CREATE TABLE prontuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    medico_id INT,
    data_consulta DATETIME,
    descricao TEXT,
    prescricao TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (medico_id) REFERENCES usuarios(id)
);
```

3. **Estilos CSS**
```css

}

}

}

}

    text-decoration: none;
    padding: 10px 15px;
}

    margin-bottom: 15px;
}

    width: 100%;
    padding: 8px;
    border: 1px solid #ddd;
    border-radius: 4px;
}

    margin: 20px 0;
}

    border: 1px solid #ddd;
    text-align: left;
}
```

4. **JavaScript Base**
```javascript
const auth = {
    async login(email, senha) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/login', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ email, senha })
            });
            
            if (response.ok) {
                const data = await response.json();
                localStorage.setItem('token', data.token);
                window.location.href = 'dashboard.html';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
        }
    },

    verificarAuth() {
        return !!localStorage.getItem('token');
    },

    logout() {
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
        window.location.href = 'login.html';
    }
};
```

```html

    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Clínica Médica</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
</head>
<body>
    <nav class="navbar">
        <div class="container">
            <ul>
                <li><a href="index.html">Home</a></li>
                <li><a href="pages/login.html">Login</a></li>
                <li><a href="pages/agendamentos.html">Agendamentos</a></li>
            </ul>
        </div>

        <!-- Conteúdo da página inicial -->
    </div>

    <script src="js/auth.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
```

```sql
CREATE DATABASE clinica;
USE clinica;

CREATE TABLE usuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    senha VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    tipo ENUM('admin', 'medico', 'paciente')
);

CREATE TABLE pacientes (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    cpf VARCHAR(14) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    telefone VARCHAR(20),
    email VARCHAR(100),
    data_nascimento DATE
);

CREATE TABLE agendamentos (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    medico_id INT,
    data DATE NOT NULL,
    hora TIME NOT NULL,
    status ENUM('agendado', 'confirmado', 'cancelado') DEFAULT 'agendado',
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (medico_id) REFERENCES usuarios(id)
);

CREATE TABLE prontuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    data_consulta DATETIME,
    diagnostico TEXT,
    prescricao TEXT,
    observacoes TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id)
);
```

#### Implementação:

```sql
CREATE DATABASE clinica;
USE clinica;

CREATE TABLE usuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    senha VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    tipo ENUM('admin', 'medico', 'paciente')
);

CREATE TABLE pacientes (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    cpf VARCHAR(14) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    telefone VARCHAR(20),
    data_nascimento DATE
);

CREATE TABLE agendamentos (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    medico_id INT,
    data DATE NOT NULL,
    hora TIME NOT NULL,
    status ENUM('pendente', 'confirmado', 'cancelado') DEFAULT 'pendente',
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (medico_id) REFERENCES usuarios(id)
);

CREATE TABLE prontuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    medico_id INT,
    data_consulta DATETIME,
    diagnostico TEXT,
    prescricao TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (medico_id) REFERENCES usuarios(id)
);
```

```javascript
const auth = {
    token: localStorage.getItem('token'),

    async login(email, senha) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/login', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ email, senha })
            });
            
            if (response.ok) {
                const data = await response.json();
                this.setToken(data.token);
                window.location.href = 'dashboard.html';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
        }
    },

    setToken(token) {
        this.token = token;
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
    },

    logout() {
        this.token = null;
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
        window.location.href = 'login.html';
    },

    isAuthenticated() {
        return !!this.token;
    }
};
```

```html
            <div class="form-group">
                <input type="email" id="email" placeholder="Email" required>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
                <input type="password" id="senha" placeholder="Senha" required>
            </div>
            <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">Entrar</button>
        </form>
    </div>
    <script src="../js/auth.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
```

```javascript
const auth = {
    token: localStorage.getItem('token'),

    async login(email, senha) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/login', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ email, senha })
            });
            
            if (response.ok) {
                const data = await response.json();
                this.setToken(data.token);
                window.location.href = 'dashboard.html';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
        }
    },

    setToken(token) {
        this.token = token;
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
    },

    logout() {
        this.token = null;
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
        window.location.href = 'login.html';
    }
};

document.getElementById('loginForm')?.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const email = document.getElementById('email').value;
    const senha = document.getElementById('senha').value;
    await auth.login(email, senha);
});
```

```javascript
const pacienteService = {
    async listar() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/pacientes', {
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${auth.token}`
                }
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao listar pacientes:', error);
        }
    },

    async cadastrar(paciente) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/pacientes', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${auth.token}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(paciente)
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao cadastrar paciente:', error);
        }
    }
};
```

### Passo 2: Banco de Dados

```sql
CREATE DATABASE clinica;
USE clinica;

CREATE TABLE usuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    senha VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    tipo ENUM('admin', 'medico', 'paciente')
);

CREATE TABLE pacientes (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    cpf VARCHAR(14) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    telefone VARCHAR(20),
    data_nascimento DATE
);

CREATE TABLE agendamentos (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    medico_id INT,
    data DATE NOT NULL,
    hora TIME NOT NULL,
    status ENUM('pendente', 'confirmado', 'cancelado'),
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (medico_id) REFERENCES usuarios(id)
);

CREATE TABLE prontuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    paciente_id INT,
    medico_id INT,
    data_consulta DATETIME,
    diagnostico TEXT,
    prescricao TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (paciente_id) REFERENCES pacientes(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (medico_id) REFERENCES usuarios(id)
);
```

```javascript
const prontuarioService = {
    async listar(pacienteId) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`/api/prontuarios/${pacienteId}`, {
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${auth.token}`
                }
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao listar prontuários:', error);
        }
    },

    async criar(prontuario) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/prontuarios', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${auth.token}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(prontuario)
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao criar prontuário:', error);
        }
    }
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    carregarProntuarios();
});
```

```sql
DELIMITER //

CREATE PROCEDURE sp_criar_prontuario(
    IN p_paciente_id INT,
    IN p_medico_id INT,
    IN p_diagnostico TEXT,
    IN p_prescricao TEXT
)
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO prontuarios (
        paciente_id, 
        medico_id, 
        data_consulta,
        diagnostico,
        prescricao
    ) VALUES (
        p_paciente_id,
        p_medico_id,
        NOW(),
        p_diagnostico,
        p_prescricao
    );
END //

DELIMITER ;
```

#### 2. JavaScript Dashboard

```javascript
const dashboard = {
    async init() {
        await this.carregarEstatisticas();
        this.bindEvents();
    },

    async carregarEstatisticas() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/dashboard/stats', {
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${auth.token}`
                }
            });
            const stats = await response.json();
            this.atualizarDashboard(stats);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao carregar estatísticas:', error);
        }
    },

    atualizarDashboard(stats) {
        document.getElementById('totalPacientes').textContent = stats.totalPacientes;
        document.getElementById('consultasHoje').textContent = stats.consultasHoje;
        document.getElementById('agendamentosPendentes').textContent = stats.agendamentosPendentes;
    },

    bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('btnLogout').addEventListener('click', () => {
            auth.logout();
        });
    }
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    dashboard.init();
});
```

```sql
-- Índices para otimização
CREATE INDEX idx_pacientes_nome ON pacientes(nome);
CREATE INDEX idx_agendamentos_data ON agendamentos(data);
CREATE INDEX idx_prontuarios_paciente ON prontuarios(paciente_id);

-- Procedures
DELIMITER //

CREATE PROCEDURE sp_criar_agendamento(
    IN p_paciente_id INT,
    IN p_medico_id INT,
    IN p_data DATE,
    IN p_hora TIME
)
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO agendamentos (paciente_id, medico_id, data, hora, status)
    VALUES (p_paciente_id, p_medico_id, p_data, p_hora, 'pendente');
END //

-- Triggers para logs
CREATE TRIGGER trg_log_agendamento
AFTER INSERT ON agendamentos
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO logs (tabela, operacao, registro_id, data)
    VALUES ('agendamentos', 'INSERT', NEW.id, NOW());
END //

DELIMITER ;
```

```sql
        dados,
        data_hora
    ) VALUES (

        'INSERT',
```

```javascript
const NotificationService = {
    async enviarNotificacao(tipo, dados) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/notificacoes', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${auth.token}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({ tipo, dados })
            });
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao enviar notificação:', error);
        }
    },

    async notificarAgendamento(agendamento) {
        await this.enviarNotificacao('agendamento', {
            pacienteId: agendamento.paciente_id,
            data: agendamento.data,
            hora: agendamento.hora
        });
    }
};
```

```javascript
const AuthService = {
    token: null,
    
    async login(credentials) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/auth/login', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify(credentials)
            });
            
            if (response.ok) {
                const data = await response.json();
                this.setToken(data.token);
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
            return false;
        }
    },

    setToken(token) {
        this.token = token;
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
    }
};
```

```javascript
const LogService = {
    async log(action, data) {
        try {
            await fetch('/api/logs', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${AuthService.token}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    action,
                    data,
                    timestamp: new Date()
                })
            });
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao registrar log:', error);
        }
    }
};
```

```sql
CREATE DATABASE clinica;
USE clinica;

CREATE TABLE usuarios (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    senha VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    tipo ENUM('admin', 'medico', 'paciente')
);

CREATE TABLE pacientes (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    nome VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    cpf VARCHAR(14) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    telefone VARCHAR(20),
    data_nascimento DATE
);
```

GitHub Copilot: ### Plano: Sistema Clínica - Login e Autenticação

1. **Estrutura**
- Criar auth.js
- Implementar funções de autenticação
- Gerenciar sessão do usuário

```javascript
const auth = {
    token: localStorage.getItem('token'),

    async login(email, senha) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/login', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ email, senha })
            });
            
            if (response.ok) {
                const data = await response.json();
                this.setToken(data.token);
                window.location.href = '../pages/dashboard.html';
            } else {
                alert('Email ou senha inválidos');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro no login:', error);
            alert('Erro ao fazer login');
        }
    },

    setToken(token) {
        this.token = token;
        localStorage.setItem('token', token);
    },

    logout() {
        this.token = null;
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
        window.location.href = '../index.html';
    },

    isAuthenticated() {
        return !!this.token;
    }
};

// Event Listeners
document.getElementById('formLogin')?.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const email = document.getElementById('email').value;
    const senha = document.getElementById('senha').value;
    await auth.login(email, senha);
});
```
